 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:10%;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;">Item&#160;5.02 </td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Departure of Directors or Principal Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Principal Officers.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On November&#160;18, 2019, the Board of Directors (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> US, Inc. <span style="white-space:nowrap">(&#8220;T-Mobile&#8221;</span> or the &#8220;Company&#8221;), following a multi-year, comprehensive leadership succession planning process, announced that G. Michael Sievert, age 50, has been appointed as Chief Executive Officer (&#8220;CEO&#8221;) of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> effective as of May&#160;1, 2020. John Legere, the current CEO, will cease to serve as CEO of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> effective as of April&#160;30, 2020, upon the conclusion of his current employment agreement with <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</span> Mr.&#160;Legere will continue to serve as CEO of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and as a member of the Board through such date, and will continue to serve as a member of the Board thereafter. In connection with Mr.&#160;Sievert&#8217;s appointment as CEO, on and effective as of November&#160;15, 2019, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> entered into an employment agreement (the &#8220;Sievert Employment Agreement&#8221;) with Mr.&#160;Sievert, which supersedes and replaces the prior compensation term sheet between <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and Mr.&#160;Sievert, dated as of January&#160;1, 2017, as amended. Information regarding Mr.&#160;Sievert&#8217;s business experience, qualifications and other biographical data, including his experience over the past five years, is incorporated by reference to <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> Definitive Proxy Statement relating to <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> 2019 Annual Meeting of Stockholders, filed on Schedule 14A with the Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#8220;SEC&#8221;) on April&#160;26, 2019. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">In addition, (i)&#160;on November&#160;15, 2019, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> adopted a third amendment to the amended and restated employment agreement, dated as of December&#160;20, 2017, with J. Braxton Carter, the Company&#8217;s Executive Vice President and Chief Financial Officer (the &#8220;Carter Amendment&#8221;) and (ii)&#160;on November&#160;14, 2019, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> adopted a Compensation Term Sheet with Neville Ray, currently the Company&#8217;s Executive Vice President and Chief Technology Officer (the &#8220;Ray Term Sheet&#8221;). The Carter Amendment and the Ray Term Sheet each became effective as of November&#160;15, 2019. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The material terms of the Sievert Employment Agreement, the Carter Amendment and the Ray Term Sheet are described below. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">Sievert Employment Agreement </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">Pursuant to the Sievert Employment Agreement, Mr.&#160;Sievert will continue to serve as <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> President and Chief Operating Officer through April&#160;30, 2020. Effective May&#160;1, 2020, Mr.&#160;Sievert will serve as <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> President and CEO. The Sievert Employment Agreement provides for an initial employment term through the third anniversary of the date on which Mr.&#160;Sievert becomes CEO, subject to automatic one (1)-year extensions thereafter unless at least ninety (90)&#160;days&#8217; prior notice of <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-renewal</span> is given by either party. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">Pursuant to the Sievert Employment Agreement, Mr.&#160;Sievert is entitled to (i)&#160;an annual base salary initially equal to $1,200,000, which will automatically increase to (a) $1,400,000 effective as of January&#160;1, 2020, (b) $1,500,000 effective as of January&#160;1, 2021 and (c)&#160;the greater of (x) $1,600,000 or (y)&#160;the then-current median annual base salary for chief executive officers in <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> then-current peer group (the &#8220;Peer Group&#8221;) effective as of January&#160;1, 2022; (ii) commencing with calendar year 2020, an annual short-term incentive (&#8220;STI&#8221;) targeted at 250% of his base salary (with a maximum award equal to 200% of target), payable based on the attainment of <span style="white-space:nowrap">pre-established</span>&#160;performance goals; and (iii)&#160;employee benefits to the same extent and on the same terms as such benefits are provided generally by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> to its senior executives. Following the date on which Mr.&#160;Sievert becomes CEO, he is also eligible for a <span style="white-space:nowrap">one-time</span> cash payment of $3,500,000 (the &#8220;Retention Payment&#8221;), payable on or within thirty (30)&#160;days following the earlier to occur of (a)&#160;the date on which the transactions contemplated by the Business Combination Agreement, dated April&#160;29, 2018, between <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> Sprint Corporation and certain other parties named therein (collectively, the &#8220;Transaction&#8221;) close, (b)&#160;the date on which the Transaction is abandoned or terminated or (c)&#160;December&#160;1, 2020, subject to Mr.&#160;Sievert&#8217;s continued employment through such date. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">Pursuant to the Sievert Employment Agreement, commencing with calendar year 2020, Mr.&#160;Sievert will be entitled to annual long-term incentive awards (&#8220;LTI awards&#8221;) with a target grant-date value (the &#8220;Annual LTI Target Value&#8221;) that is no less than $13,500,000, which will be allocated as follows: 50% of such value will be granted in the form of performance-based restricted stock units (&#8220;PRSUs&#8221;) and the remaining 50% of such value will be granted in the form of time-based restricted stock units (&#8220;RSUs&#8221;). Mr.&#160;Sievert&#8217;s Annual LTI Target Value will automatically increase to (i) $14,250,000 for LTI awards granted during 2021 and (ii)&#160;for LTI awards granted on or after January&#160;1, 2022, the greater of (a) $15,000,000 and (b)&#160;the then-current median target grant-date value of annual equity incentive awards for chief executive officers in <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> then-current Peer Group. With respect to 60% of the total time-based RSUs granted to Mr.&#160;Sievert as annual LTI awards during each of calendar years 2020, 2021 and 2022 (<span style="font-style:Italic">i.e.</span>, 30% of the total Annual LTI Target Value for each such year), the total length of the vesting schedule of such RSUs will be no longer than the length of the median total length of the vesting schedules of annual time-based equity incentive awards for chief executive officers in <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> then-current Peer Group at the time of grant. </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:0"></p>
 </div>

 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">In connection with his commencement as CEO, within fifteen (15)&#160;days following the date on which Mr.&#160;Sievert becomes CEO, Mr.&#160;Sievert will be granted a<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;one-time</span>&#160;award of PRSUs (the &#8220;Special PRSUs&#8221;) under the Company&#8217;s 2013 Omnibus Incentive Plan (as amended, the &#8220;Plan&#8221;), with respect to a target number of shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> common stock equal to the quotient of $20,000,000 divided by the average closing price of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> common stock over the period commencing on November&#160;18, 2019 and ending on the date on which Mr.&#160;Sievert becomes CEO (such average closing price, the &#8220;Starting Price&#8221;). The Special PRSUs will cliff-vest on the third anniversary of the date on which Mr.&#160;Sievert becomes CEO, based on <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> total shareholder return relative to its then-current Peer Group during the applicable performance period and subject to Mr.&#160;Sievert&#8217;s continued employment through such date (except as otherwise noted below and in the PRSU award agreement). In order for more than 100% of the target number of Special PRSUs to vest, there must be at least a 20% increase in <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> stock price during the period beginning on the date on which Mr.&#160;Sievert becomes CEO (with <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> stock price as of such date deemed to equal the Starting Price) and ending on the vesting date (with <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> stock price as of such date determined based on the average closing price of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> common stock over the thirty <span style="white-space:nowrap">(30)-day</span> period preceding such vesting date). </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The Sievert Employment Agreement provides that if Mr.&#160;Sievert&#8217;s employment is terminated by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> other than for &#8220;cause&#8221; (as defined in the Sievert Employment Agreement), by Mr.&#160;Sievert for &#8220;good reason&#8221; (as defined in the Sievert Employment Agreement), or due to <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span><span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;non-renewal</span>&#160;of the Sievert Employment Agreement (each, a &#8220;qualifying termination&#8221;), then, subject to his timely execution and<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;non-revocation</span>&#160;of a release, he will be entitled to receive: </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt"></p>

the Sievert Employment Agreement, a copy of which will be subsequently filed with the SEC. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">The Carter Amendment amends Mr.&#160;Carter&#8217;s employment agreement to (i)&#160;extend the term of Mr.&#160;Carter&#8217;s employment thereunder through July&#160;1, 2020 (the &#8220;Expiration Date&#8221;) and (ii)&#160;clarify that Mr.&#160;Carter&#8217;s employment with <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> will automatically terminate upon the expiration of the employment term. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The Carter Amendment provides that, during the remainder of his employment term, Mr.&#160;Carter shall continue to (i)&#160;serve as Executive Vice President and Chief Financial Officer of the Company, (ii)&#160;receive the same base salary as currently in effect (i.e., $950,000 per year) and (iii)&#160;be eligible to participate in employee benefit plans maintained by the Company, in each case, in accordance with the terms and conditions of his existing employment agreement. Except as otherwise determined by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile, </span>&#32;Mr.&#160;Carter will not be eligible to receive STI awards or grants of LTI awards after December&#160;31, 2019. </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:0"></p>

 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">Pursuant to the Carter Amendment, subject to Mr.&#160;Carter&#8217;s continued employment through December&#160;31, 2019, and provided that Mr.&#160;Carter timely executes and does not revoke a release of claims in a form determined by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> that becomes effective on or before such date, Mr.&#160;Carter will receive the following payments and benefits: </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt"></p>

<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:9%;text-align:left;">&#160;</td>
<td style="width:3%;vertical-align:top;">&#8226;</td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Mr.&#160;Carter will receive an STI award for calendar year 2019, which shall be paid to Mr.&#160;Carter in a single <span style="white-space:nowrap">lump-sum </span>&#32;amount at the same time as 2019 STI awards are paid to similarly situated executives of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> (but no later than March&#160;15, 2020).</td> </tr> </table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">If Mr.&#160;Carter becomes entitled to receive the Separation Benefits and 2019 STI award as described above, he will not be entitled to any further separation payments or benefits upon his subsequent termination of employment with <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> (except as described below). </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The Carter Amendment also provides that, upon a termination of Mr.&#160;Carter&#8217;s employment due to the expiration of the employment term (or, if earlier, upon a termination without &#8220;cause&#8221; or for &#8220;good reason&#8221; (each as defined in his employment agreement)), subject to his timely execution and <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-revocation</span> of a release, he will be entitled to receive company-paid health and dental benefit coverage for up to eighteen (18)&#160;months following such termination. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">In addition, subject to Mr.&#160;Carter&#8217;s continued employment through the Expiration Date (except as otherwise described below), he will be eligible to receive a <span style="white-space:nowrap">one-time</span> cash bonus in the amount of $7,525,000 (the &#8220;Special Bonus&#8221;), payable on or within seventy-four (74)&#160;days following the Expiration Date, subject to his timely execution and<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;non-revocation</span>&#160;of a release. If Mr.&#160;Carter&#8217;s employment is terminated by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> without &#8220;cause&#8221; or due to his resignation for &#8220;good reason&#8221; between January&#160;1, 2020 and the Expiration Date, he will be entitled to receive a <span style="white-space:nowrap">pro-rated</span> Special Bonus, which shall be paid on or within seventy-four (74)&#160;days following his termination date, subject to his timely execution and<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;non-revocation</span>&#160;of a release. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The Carter Amendment further provides that, during the period commencing on January&#160;1, 2020 and ending on the date that is two (2)&#160;business days before the date on which the Company&#8217;s 2019 Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">10-K</span> is filed with the SEC (such date, the <span style="white-space:nowrap">&#8220;10-K</span> Filing Date&#8221; and such window, the &#8220;Put Window&#8221;), Mr.&#160;Carter will have the right to require that <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> purchase some or all of the vested shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> common stock then-held by him that were issued or paid to him pursuant to LTI or other equity-based awards (the &#8220;Vested Shares&#8221;), at a price per Vested Share equal to the volume weighted average price of the Company&#8217;s common stock over the thirty <span style="white-space:nowrap">(30)-day</span> period ending with (and including) the <span style="white-space:nowrap">10-K</span> Filing Date. Mr.&#160;Carter may exercise the repurchase right by delivering to the Company, during the Put Window, a written notice indicating that he is exercising the repurchase right and specifying the number of Vested Shares as to which the repurchase right is being exercised. The closing of the purchase of any Vested Shares for which Mr.&#160;Carter validly exercises his repurchase right will occur on the second (2<sup style="font-size:85%;vertical-align:top">nd</sup>) business day following the <span style="white-space:nowrap">10-K</span> Filing Date. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The foregoing description of the Carter Amendment is qualified in its entirety by the full text of the Carter Amendment, a copy of which will subsequently be filed with the SEC.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">Ray Term Sheet </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">Pursuant to the Ray Term Sheet, Mr.&#160;Ray, currently <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> Executive Vice President and Chief Technology Officer, will serve as the President, Technology of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</span> The Ray Term Sheet provides for an initial two (2)-year employment term through November&#160;15, 2021 (the &#8220;Initial Term&#8221;), subject to automatic one (1)-year extensions unless at least sixty (60)&#160;days&#8217; prior notice of <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-extension</span> is given by either party. </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:0"></p>
 </div>



<p style='page-break-before:always'> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" />

 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">Pursuant to the Ray Term Sheet, Mr.&#160;Ray is entitled to (i)&#160;an annual base salary equal to $900,000, (ii) commencing with calendar year 2020, an annual STI targeted at 200% of Mr.&#160;Ray&#8217;s eligible base earnings during the applicable year, payable based on the attainment of<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;pre-established</span>&#160;performance goals, and (iii)&#160;commencing with calendar year 2020, an annual LTI award or other equity awards with a target grant-date value that is no less than $6,750,000. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The Ray Term Sheet provides that the Letter Regarding Severance Benefits between Mr.&#160;Ray and <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> dated April&#160;28, 2018 (the &#8220;Severance Letter&#8221;), will remain in effect and that Mr.&#160;Ray will be entitled to severance thereunder upon a termination of Mr.&#160;Ray&#8217;s employment by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> other than for &#8220;cause&#8221; or by Mr.&#160;Ray for &#8220;good reason&#8221; (each such term as defined in the Severance Letter) upon or within twelve (12)&#160;months following the &#8220;transaction date&#8221; (as defined in the Severance Letter). In addition, the Ray Term Sheet provides that upon a termination of Mr.&#160;Ray&#8217;s employment by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> other than for &#8220;cause&#8221; or by Mr.&#160;Ray for &#8220;good reason&#8221; at any time during the Initial Term (excluding any termination with respect to which the Severance Letter applies), subject to his timely execution and <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-revocation</span> of a release and continued compliance with certain <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-competition</span> and <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-solicitation</span> restrictions following such termination, he will be entitled to receive the severance benefits set forth in the Severance Letter, except that any accelerated vesting of his LTI awards that he becomes entitled to receive shall apply only to his existing or future annual LTI awards (and shall not apply to any special or <span style="white-space:nowrap">one-time</span> LTI awards granted on or after November&#160;15, 2019). A description of the material terms of the Severance Letter (including the severance benefits payable thereunder) was included in <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> filed with the SEC on April&#160;30, 2018, and such description is incorporated herein by reference. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">To the extent that any payment or benefit received by Mr.&#160;Ray pursuant to the Ray Term Sheet or otherwise would be subject to an excise tax under Internal Revenue Code Section&#160;4999, such payments and/or benefits will be subject to a &#8220;best pay cap&#8221; reduction if such reduction would result in a greater net<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;after-tax</span>&#160;benefit to Mr.&#160;Ray than receiving the full amount of such payments. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The foregoing description of the Ray Term Sheet is qualified in its entirety by the full text of the Ray Term Sheet, a copy of which will subsequently be filed with the SEC. </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:10%;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;">Item&#160;7.01 </td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Regulation FD Disclosure.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On November&#160;18, 2019, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> issued a press release announcing that Mr.&#160;Legere, the current CEO, will cease to serve as CEO of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> effective as of April&#160;30, 2020, and that Mr.&#160;Sievert will succeed Mr.&#160;Legere as CEO of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> effective as of May&#160;1, 2020. A copy of the press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The information contained in Item 7.01 and the exhibit attached hereto, shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section, nor shall they be deemed incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such a filing. </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt"></p>

<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>EX-99.1</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Mike Sievert to Succeed John Legere as CEO of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> on May&nbsp;1, 2020 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><I>Mike Sievert is committed to the successful <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> strategy, demonstrating that <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> will remain a disruptive force in US wireless marketplace to benefit consumers </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><I>John Legere will continue as CEO through end of his contract on April&nbsp;30, 2020 and will focus on a smooth leadership transition and
closing the Sprint acquisition </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><I>Leadership transition is culmination of comprehensive multi-year succession planning process
led by John Legere and the Board of Directors for next generation of leadership </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>BELLEVUE, Wash. (November 18, 2019)</B> &#150; <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US, Inc. (NASDAQ: TMUS) today announced that its Board of Directors has named Mike Sievert as Chief Executive Officer, effective May&nbsp;1, 2020. Currently President, Chief Operating Officer and a Board
Director, Sievert will assume the CEO role from John Legere after the conclusion of Legere&#146;s contract on April&nbsp;30, 2020. Sievert&#146;s new title will be President and CEO. Legere will remain a member of the Board. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The CEO transition is part of the Board&#146;s well-established succession planning process to position the next generation of leadership at <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> to take the Company forward. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;John Legere has had an enormously successful run as CEO. As the architect
of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> strategy and the company&#146;s complete transformation, John has put <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US in an incredibly strong position. I have the highest respect for his
performance as a manager and as a friend, I am very grateful to him for the time together,&#148; said Tim H&ouml;ttges, Deutsche Telekom CEO, and Chairman of the Board of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US. &#147;John taught
everyone at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> that if you listen to customers and empower employees, you can change a culture &#150; and by doing so &#150; change a company and an entire industry. On behalf of the Board of Directors,
I would like to thank John, and of course Mike, and all the employees for everything they have achieved over the past seven years. We have tremendous respect for John&#146;s leadership and appreciate his incredible contributions to <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> success. The Board is pleased that John will support this leadership transition while focusing on closing our pending acquisition of Sprint.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">With Legere&#146;s involvement, the Board undertook a comprehensive, multi-year,&nbsp;leadership succession planning process tied to the strategic direction
of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and has chosen Sievert to step into the CEO role next Spring. Sievert has worked alongside Legere for the last seven years, transforming <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> into the
fastest growing wireless provider in the market and ultimately into the tremendously successful <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier.</FONT> As <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> Chief Marketing Officer and then COO,
Sievert led the design and execution of the 16 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> &#147;moves&#148; that have defined the company and established <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> as the customer satisfaction leader
and most-loved brand in the industry. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Today, in his current role as President and COO, Sievert leads a team of tens of thousands of
customer-focused disruptors and innovators who are changing the rules of wireless every day. He leads all of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> marketing and product groups, and all retail, sales, and customer support groups for
all of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> segments and brands, among other responsibilities. In addition, over the past two years he has worked closely with Legere on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT>
merger planning, integration, and regulatory approval initiatives, with the goal of creating the New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> by successfully closing the pending acquisition of Sprint. Sievert has also served as a member of
the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Board of Directors for nearly 2 years. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sievert and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT>
are dedicated to continuing and supercharging the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> strategy as the New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;I have had the opportunity to get to know Mike both personally and professionally over our years of working together, and I am very pleased to be
welcoming him to his impending new role,&#148; commented Tim H&ouml;ttges. &#147;He has been actively involved in all our most important corporate decisions since he joined <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> in 2012. Mike is an
experienced, passionate, and results-oriented leader, who cares deeply about our employees and customers and lives the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> values of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> brand every day.
He has the support of John Legere and the full confidence of the Board.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;I hired Mike in 2012 and I have great confidence in him. I have
mentored him as he took on increasingly broad responsibilities, and he is absolutely the right choice as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> next CEO,&#148; said John Legere. &#147;Mike is well prepared to lead <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> into the future. He has a deep understanding of where <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> has been and where it needs to go to remain the most innovative company in the industry. I am extremely
proud of the culture and enthusiasm we have built around challenging the status quo and our ongoing commitment to putting customers first. Together, these attributes have distinguished <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> in the
marketplace and on Wall Street, giving us a powerful business advantage that is instilled throughout every level of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT> I am confident it will thrive under Mike&#146;s leadership.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;In the months ahead, my focus will be on ensuring a smooth leadership transition and continuing to work closely with the Board and Mike to complete the
Sprint transaction,&#148; added John Legere. &#147;This merger will create the New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> &#150; a company that is uniquely positioned to continue disrupting the wireless category &#150; and beyond. This
marks the beginning of a dynamic new chapter for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.&#148;</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;I am very grateful to Tim and the Board
for this exciting opportunity to lead <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> into the future,&#148; commented Mike Sievert. &#147;I personally want to thank John for all he has done for me and for the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> brand, our customers, employees, partners, and investors. John is a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-of-a-kind,</FONT></FONT></FONT> visionary leader who has redefined the role of CEO and demonstrated how to use it to create positive change for
customers, employees, and investors alike. I have been fortunate to work together with him to build <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> purpose-driven strategy to address customer pain points, an approach that has been the
foundation for our unprecedented growth.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> culture, which all our employees live every
day, will not change,&#148; continued Mike Sievert. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;T-Mobile</FONT> is not just about one individual. Our company is built around an extraordinarily capable management team and thousands of talented, committed,
and customer-obsessed employees. Going forward, my mission is to build on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> industry-leading reputation for empowering employees to deliver an outstanding customer experience and to position <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> not only as the leading mobile carrier, but as one of the most admired companies in America.&#148; </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US, Inc. </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As America&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier,</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US, Inc. (NASDAQ: TMUS) is redefining
the way consumers and businesses buy wireless services through leading product and service innovation. Our advanced nationwide 4G LTE network delivers outstanding wireless experiences to 84.2&nbsp;million customers who are unwilling to compromise on
quality and value. Based in Bellevue, Washington, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US provides services through its subsidiaries and operates its flagship brands, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Metro by <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT> For more information, please visit <U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">http://www.t-mobile.com</FONT></U>. </P>
